msg:Advantages: The front desk service is good. The girl who checked in on the first day upgraded my room for free and took the initiative to add me on WeChat to inform me of the surrounding business and dining conditions) and the boy who checked out on the second day (after listening to my complaints about the hygiene conditions, he took the initiative to send us snacks) had good service attitudes.
Disadvantages: The hygiene is really not good. This is the first time I doubt this level of hygiene. First of all, when I entered the door, I saw the sofa in circles and it felt very dirty. I called the cleaning staff, and she said that there was a wedding banquet on the day before I checked in, and they lived here the day before. Maybe it was the child's urine. Later, she called the front desk again. The front desk said that it was not the child's urine, but the circle that was naturally produced after they cleaned the sofa. No matter what it was, we gave up sitting on the sofa. The explanation of the situation was also to inform the hotel that it was not us. Then there was the bed. The pillow had a very strange smell, and the quilt was so hard that I really didn't want to touch it. But because I had reported the sofa issue before, I was worried that calling the cleaning staff would make the hotel think it was too much trouble, so I just endured it. Fortunately, it was not cold, and I barely made do without the quilt. I really couldn't sleep all night, and I checked out quickly at 6 o'clock in the morning.
